msg:Snow Garden Hotel is almost a ******* Museum: on almost every wall is something of cultural interest.
As is so often the case in  China the group of young women on reception duties band together to help the linguistically challenged foreign tourist.
The hotel is situated in Jinzhu Town, which is about half way between Daocheng Airport and Yading Scenic Area, helpful for acclimatisation. It is on one of the main streets, with easy access to shops and eateries.

name:Wâ€iâ€lâ€lâ€iâ€aâ€mâ€gâ€râ€aâ€yâ€8â€1
info:Comfy Double Room
info:Stayed in June 2022
info:Couples
info:47 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted June 26, 2022
msg:Really nice hotel conveniently located near restaurants and museum. Good place to stay if passing through to Yading, Kaeding, or Chengdu. The hotel has a decent breakfast with a variety of options, all Chinese. 

The hotsprings were closed when I was there due to the government having a meeting the next day. Why they couldn't have them opened made no sense, but it costs extra to utilize them anyway. 

The rooms are equipped with oxygen pumps for 100 RMB a day if you need. The elevation is around 4100 meters so if not acclimatized could be an issue. 

Rooms are modern, very large, and include comfortable beds, large TV with hundreds of channels, for free, but very common in many Chinese hotels. 

Bathrooms are large with separated showers and toilets, as well as sink and mirror. Overall a very quality room with American standard. Highly recommend for a night. 

Great hotpot restaurants nearby and other options.

msg:It feels like a super good hotel, with diffuse oxygen supply. For 100 yuan, there is oxygen supply from check-in in the evening to nine o'clock in the morning of the next day, which can reduce the equivalent altitude to 2800. People feel much better all of a sudden, and it is also equipped with a humidifier, which is very powerful. The plateau is very dry, and the body will feel better with a humidifier. The room is also very clean, beautifully decorated, and the murals and paintings are very exquisite. There is also a free oxygen room in the sales depar**ent on the first floor of the hotel. The service of the young lady is also very thoughtful, and the oxygen is sufficient. Of course, the hot spring hotel also has to talk about the hot springs â™¨ï¸, but it's a pity that I was too tired to rush, so I didn't go, leaving some regrets. What I am a little dissatisfied with is that the water pipe under the bathroom basin leaked, and I wet my slippers unknowingly. Overall, I feel that the hotel is very good. I came back from Aden and wanted to stay for one night on the way back, but later the itinerary was adjusted. The breakfast is very average, nothing special.
